    4913             : 
    4914             : /**
    4915             :  * Pushed floats are floats whose placeholders are in a previous
    4916             :  * continuation.  They might themselves be next-continuations of a float
    4917             :  * that partially fit in an earlier continuation, or they might be the
    4918             :  * first continuation of a float that couldn't be placed at all.
    4919             :  *
    4920             :  * Pushed floats live permanently at the beginning of a block's float
    4921             :  * list, where they must live *before* any floats whose placeholders are
    4922             :  * in that block.
    4923             :  *
    4924             :  * Temporarily, during reflow, they also live on the pushed floats list,
    4925             :  * which only holds them between (a) when one continuation pushes them to
    4926             :  * its pushed floats list because they don't fit and (b) when the next
    4927             :  * continuation pulls them onto the beginning of its float list.
    4928             :  *
    4929             :  * DrainPushedFloats sets up pushed floats the way we need them at the
    4930             :  * start of reflow; they are then reflowed by ReflowPushedFloats (which
    4931             :  * might push some of them on).  Floats with placeholders in this block
    4932             :  * are reflowed by (BlockReflowInput/nsLineLayout)::AddFloat, which
    4933             :  * also maintains these invariants.
    4934             :  *
    4935             :  * DrainSelfPushedFloats moves any pushed floats from this block's own
    4936             :  * PushedFloats list back into mFloats.  DrainPushedFloats additionally
    4937             :  * moves frames from its prev-in-flow's PushedFloats list into mFloats.
    4938             :  */
    4939             : void
